		<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><div class="shortdescription nomobile noexcerpt noprint searchaux" style="display:none">Spanish association football player</div>

</p>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">In this <a href="/wiki/Spanish_name" class="mw-redirect" title="Spanish name">Spanish name</a>, the first or paternal&#32;<a href="/wiki/Surname" title="Surname">surname</a> is <i> Jiménez</i>&#32;and the second or maternal family name is <i>  Silva</i>.</div>

<td style="text-align:center;vertical-align:middle;"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/2004_UEFA_European_Under-19_Championship" title="2004 UEFA European Under-19 Championship">2004 Switzerland</a></span></td>
<td style="text-align:center;vertical-align:middle;">
</td></tr></tbody></table>
</div></div></th></tr><tr><td colspan="4" style="text-align:center;color:darkslategray; font-size:95%">
* Senior club appearances and goals counted for the domestic league only&#32;and correct as of 7 March 2021</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><b>David Josué Jiménez Silva</b> (<small>Spanish pronunciation:&#160;</small><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Spanish" title="Help:IPA/Spanish">[daið sila]</a></span>; born 8 January 1986) is a Spanish professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">footballer</a> who plays for <a href="/wiki/La_Liga" title="La Liga">La Liga</a> club <a href="/wiki/Real_Sociedad" title="Real Sociedad">Real Sociedad</a>. Silva plays mainly as a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Central_midfielder" title="Midfielder">central</a> or an <a href="/wiki/Attacking_midfielder" class="mw-redirect" title="Attacking midfielder">attacking midfielder</a> but can also play as a <a href="/wiki/Left_winger" class="mw-redirect" title="Left winger">winger</a> or <a href="/wiki/Second_striker" class="mw-redirect" title="Second striker">second striker</a>. He is predominantly a <a href="/wiki/Left-footed" class="mw-redirect" title="Left-footed">left-footed</a> player<sup id="cite_ref-How_Pellegrini_will_seek_to_get_the_best_out_of_City&#39;s_wide_men_3-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-How_Pellegrini_will_seek_to_get_the_best_out_of_City&#39;s_wide_men-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> and his passing ability and possession-retaining qualities have earned him the nicknames "<a href="/wiki/Merlin" title="Merlin">Merlin</a>" and "El Mago" from his teammates and fans.<sup id="cite_ref-David_Silva,_or_is_it_Merlin?_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-David_Silva,_or_is_it_Merlin?-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-HBD_Merlin_5-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBD_Merlin-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> He is considered by some<sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Manual_of_Style/Words_to_watch#Unsupported_attributions" title="Wikipedia:Manual of Style/Words to watch"><span title="The material near this tag possibly uses too-vague attribution or weasel words. (March 2021)">who?</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> to be one of the best midfielders of his generation, and one of the greatest midfielders in the history of the Premier League.<sup id="cite_ref-best_central_midfielders_6-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-best_central_midfielders-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Premier_Leagues_best_ever_midfielders_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Premier_Leagues_best_ever_midfielders-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Silva spent six years of his professional career with <a href="/wiki/Valencia_CF" title="Valencia CF">Valencia CF</a>, appearing in more than 160 games and winning a <a href="/wiki/Copa_del_Rey" title="Copa del Rey">Copa del Rey</a> in <a href="/wiki/2007%E2%80%9308_Copa_del_Rey" title="200708 Copa del Rey">2008</a>. In the summer of 2010, he moved to Manchester City and has since appeared in over 400 matches.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> With them he has won two <a href="/wiki/FA_Cup" title="FA Cup">FA Cups</a>, five <a href="/wiki/EFL_Cup" title="EFL Cup">League Cups</a> and four <a href="/wiki/Premier_League_trophy" class="mw-redirect" title="Premier League trophy">Premier League</a> titles. He is regarded as one of Manchester City's greatest ever players alongside <a href="/wiki/Billy_Meredith" title="Billy Meredith">Billy Meredith</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bert_Trautmann" title="Bert Trautmann">Bert Trautmann</a>, <a href="/wiki/Colin_Bell" title="Colin Bell">Colin Bell</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sergio_Ag%C3%BCero" title="Sergio Agüero">Sergio Agüero</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> Silva has been named in the <a href="/wiki/PFA_Team_of_the_Year" title="PFA Team of the Year">PFA Team of the Year</a> three times. On 26 June 2019, Silva announced that he would leave Manchester City at the end of the <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_Manchester_City_F.C._season" title="201920 Manchester City F.C. season">201920</a> season, ending his ten-season tenure at the club.<sup id="cite_ref-:0_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> On 28 September 2019, he became the youngest player to reach 200 wins in the Premier league, breaking the record set by Chelsea defender John Terry.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Silva also represented <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_football_team" title="Spain national football team">Spain</a>, from his debut for the senior team in 2006 until his international retirement in 2018. He formed a midfield partnership with <a href="/wiki/Xavi" title="Xavi">Xavi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Andr%C3%A9s_Iniesta" title="Andrés Iniesta">Andrés Iniesta</a> which led to three consecutive international tournament victories  <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2008" title="UEFA Euro 2008">UEFA Euro 2008</a>, <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2010 FIFA World Cup">2010 FIFA World Cup</a>, and <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012" title="UEFA Euro 2012">UEFA Euro 2012</a>.  He is one of 13 <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_football_team#Most_capped_players" title="Spain national football team">Spanish players to have amassed 100 caps</a>, he scored 35 goals in his international career, making him the <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_football_team#Top_goalscorers" title="Spain national football team">4th highest goalscorer in Spain's history</a>, and also provided 29 assists, making him the second-highest assist provider in Spain's history.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_life">Early life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=David_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Early life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Silva was born in <a href="/wiki/Arguinegu%C3%ADn" title="Arguineguín">Arguineguín</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gran_Canaria" title="Gran Canaria">Gran Canaria</a>, <a href="/wiki/Canary_Islands" title="Canary Islands">Canary Islands</a>, to Fernando Jiménez, a former municipal police officer who eventually was responsible for the safety of the <a href="/wiki/Valencia_CF" title="Valencia CF">Valencia CF</a> stadium and Eva Silva. His father, Fernando, is <a href="/wiki/Spaniards" title="Spaniards">Spanish</a> (Canarian) while his mother, Eva, is of Japanese descent, claimed by the Canarian media.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Silva began playing football in the youth team of UD San Fernando, near <a href="/wiki/Maspalomas" title="Maspalomas">Maspalomas</a>. Originally, he played as a <a href="/wiki/Goalkeeper_(association_football)" title="Goalkeeper (association football)">goalkeeper</a>, before becoming a <a href="/wiki/Winger_(association_football)" class="mw-redirect" title="Winger (association football)">winger</a> and mirrored his game around his footballing idol as a youth, <a href="/wiki/Michael_Laudrup" title="Michael Laudrup">Michael Laudrup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> When he was 14, he received an offer to become a youth player at <a href="/wiki/Valencia_CF" title="Valencia CF">Valencia CF</a>, which he accepted. He stayed in Valencia's youth set-up until he was 17.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_career">Club career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=David_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Club career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Valencia">Valencia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=David_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Valencia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>A product of <a href="/wiki/Valencia_CF" title="Valencia CF">Valencia</a>'s youth system, Silva made his professional debut in <a href="/wiki/2004%E2%80%9305_Segunda_Divisi%C3%B3n" title="200405 Segunda División">200405</a>, with <a href="/wiki/Segunda_Divisi%C3%B3n" title="Segunda División">Segunda División</a>'s <a href="/wiki/SD_Eibar" title="SD Eibar">Eibar</a>, while on loan from Valencia, playing 35 league games and scoring on five occasions. In the <a href="/wiki/2005%E2%80%9306_La_Liga" title="200506 La Liga">following season</a>, he was again out on loan, this time to <a href="/wiki/Celta_de_Vigo" class="mw-redirect" title="Celta de Vigo">Celta de Vigo</a>, where he played 34 matches, scoring four goals. After two late <a href="/wiki/Substitute_(association_football)" title="Substitute (association football)">substitute</a> appearances, the first in a 20 home win over <a href="/wiki/M%C3%A1laga_CF" title="Málaga CF">Málaga</a> on 28 August 2005, Silva finished as an undisputed starter as the <a href="/wiki/Galicia_(Spain)" title="Galicia (Spain)">Galician</a> side reached the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Europa_League" title="UEFA Europa League">UEFA Cup</a> straight from the second-tier.
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:David_Silva_vs_Newcastle.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/David_Silva_vs_Newcastle.jpg/220px-David_Silva_vs_Newcastle.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="215" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/David_Silva_vs_Newcastle.jpg/330px-David_Silva_vs_Newcastle.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/David_Silva_vs_Newcastle.jpg/440px-David_Silva_vs_Newcastle.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1600" data-file-height="1567" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:David_Silva_vs_Newcastle.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Silva playing for Valencia</div></div></div><p>Silva returned to Valencia in the summer of 2006, becoming an automatic first-choice despite his young age of 20. In two seasons combined, he only missed six matches and netted 14 goals, his first league goal coming on 5 November 2006 in a 11 draw at <a href="/wiki/RCD_Espanyol" title="RCD Espanyol">Espanyol</a>. In August 2008, he extended his contract by five years, amidst interest of several <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> teams.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> He won the <a href="/wiki/2007%E2%80%9308_Copa_del_Rey" title="200708 Copa del Rey">Copa del Rey 2008</a>, his first title in <a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">Spain</a>.
</p><p>After not appearing in the first three months of <a href="/wiki/2008%E2%80%9309_La_Liga" title="200809 La Liga">200809</a> due to a chronic <a href="/wiki/Ankle" title="Ankle">ankle</a> ailment,<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> Silva returned to the call-ups in mid-December. On 3 January 2009, he scored twice in a 31 home win over <a href="/wiki/Atl%C3%A9tico_Madrid" title="Atlético Madrid">Atlético Madrid</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> still contributing with 19 matches (four goals) as the <i>Che</i> qualified for the <a href="/wiki/2009%E2%80%9310_UEFA_Europa_League" title="200910 UEFA Europa League">Europa League</a>.
</p><p>In the <a href="/wiki/2009%E2%80%9310_La_Liga" title="200910 La Liga">200910 season</a>, Silva scored a career-best eight goals, as Valencia finished in third position and <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_UEFA_Champions_League" title="201011 UEFA Champions League">returned</a> to the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a>. On 15 April 2010, he scored a brace against <a href="/wiki/Athletic_Bilbao" title="Athletic Bilbao">Athletic Bilbao</a> for a 20 home win,<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> adding three assists in the 44 thriller at <a href="/wiki/SV_Werder_Bremen" title="SV Werder Bremen">Werder Bremen</a> for the Europa League's <a href="/wiki/2009%E2%80%9310_UEFA_Europa_League" title="200910 UEFA Europa League">round of 16</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Manchester_City">Manchester City</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=David_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Manchester City">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="2010.E2.80.9311_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201011_season">201011 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=David_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: 201011 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:142px;"><a href="/wiki/File:David_Silva.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6e/David_Silva.jpg/140px-David_Silva.jpg" decoding="async" width="140" height="248" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6e/David_Silva.jpg/209px-David_Silva.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/6/6e/David_Silva.jpg 2x" data-file-width="248" data-file-height="440" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:David_Silva.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Silva with Manchester City in April 2011</div></div></div>
<p>On 30 June 2010, <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City_F.C." title="Manchester City F.C.">Manchester City</a> announced that they had reached an agreement with Valencia over the transfer of Silva and that he would join the club on a four-year deal, prior to the start of the <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_Premier_League" title="201011 Premier League">201011 season</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> On 14 July, the Premier League side completed the signing<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> and Silva was awarded the number 21 shirt, the same number he wore for Valencia and when playing for <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_football_team" title="Spain national football team">Spain</a>. Manchester City had previously tried to sign Silva and his Valencia teammate <a href="/wiki/David_Villa" title="David Villa">David Villa</a> in 2008, but were put off when Valencia quoted a £135&#160;million combined price tag on both players.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>City manager <a href="/wiki/Roberto_Mancini" title="Roberto Mancini">Roberto Mancini</a> mainly deployed Silva as a winger<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> and later in a <a href="/wiki/Trequartista" class="mw-redirect" title="Trequartista">trequartista</a> role in his first season.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> Silva made his <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> debut on 14 August 2010 in a 00 draw against <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C." title="Tottenham Hotspur F.C.">Tottenham Hotspur</a> at <a href="/wiki/White_Hart_Lane" title="White Hart Lane">White Hart Lane</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> He scored his first goal for the club on 16 September, eight minutes into the <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_UEFA_Europa_League" title="201011 UEFA Europa League">Europa League group match</a> against <a href="/wiki/FC_Red_Bull_Salzburg" title="FC Red Bull Salzburg">Red Bull Salzburg</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> On 17 October, he scored his first league goal in a game against <a href="/wiki/Blackpool_F.C." title="Blackpool F.C.">Blackpool</a>, netting City's third goal in a 32 away win.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> In a 31 home win in the <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_UEFA_Europa_League" title="201011 UEFA Europa League">Europa League</a> against <a href="/wiki/Lech_Pozna%C5%84" title="Lech Pozna">Lech Pozna</a>, he set up two goals for <a href="/wiki/Emmanuel_Adebayor" title="Emmanuel Adebayor">Emmanuel Adebayor</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> He made another assist slipping through <a href="/wiki/Adam_Johnson_(footballer)" title="Adam Johnson (footballer)">Adam Johnson</a> for Manchester City's third in a 31 away win against <a href="/wiki/West_Ham_United_F.C." title="West Ham United F.C.">West Ham United</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> Erroneous media reports emerged suggesting Silva could return to Spain and cited homesickness and difficulty to adapt to the English game.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> His performances, however, impressed City <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City_F.C._supporters" title="Manchester City F.C. supporters">supporters</a> and earned him three consecutive Manchester City Player of the Month awards from October to December 2010.<sup id="cite_ref-Hat-trick_33-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hat-trick-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 12 February 2011, he was credited for the equalising goal in the 21 loss to rivals <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a> when an <a href="/wiki/Edin_D%C5%BEeko" title="Edin Deko">Edin Deko</a> shot deflected off his back and into the net. On 2 March, he scored from 20 yards out in an <a href="/wiki/FA_Cup" title="FA Cup">FA Cup</a> win (30) against <a href="/wiki/Aston_Villa_F.C." title="Aston Villa F.C.">Aston Villa</a>. Three days later, he scored the only goal in Manchester City's win against <a href="/wiki/Wigan_Athletic_F.C." title="Wigan Athletic F.C.">Wigan Athletic</a>. Silva netted the third goal in City's 50 rout of <a href="/wiki/Sunderland_A.F.C." title="Sunderland A.F.C.">Sunderland</a> on 3 April. His assist to <a href="/wiki/Yaya_Tour%C3%A9" title="Yaya Touré">Yaya Touré</a> against <a href="/wiki/Everton_F.C." title="Everton F.C.">Everton</a> at <a href="/wiki/Goodison_Park" title="Goodison Park">Goodison Park</a> took Silva to 15 assists in all competitions for the season.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (October 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p><p>Following his debut season in the Premier League, Silva emerged as one of the league's finest playmakers. <a href="/wiki/Carlos_Tevez" title="Carlos Tevez">Carlos Tevez</a> lauded him as "the best signing we [Manchester City] have made."<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> Silva finished the 201011 campaign with four goals and seven assists in 35 league appearances.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2011.E2.80.9312_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201112_season">201112 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=David_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: 201112 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;"><a href="/wiki/File:SilvaLFC.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/14/SilvaLFC.jpg/150px-SilvaLFC.jpg" decoding="async" width="150" height="210" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/14/SilvaLFC.jpg/225px-SilvaLFC.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/14/SilvaLFC.jpg/300px-SilvaLFC.jpg 2x" data-file-width="458" data-file-height="640" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:SilvaLFC.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Silva prior to a league match against Liverpool in 2011</div></div></div>
<p>Silva began the <a href="/wiki/2011%E2%80%9312_Premier_League" title="201112 Premier League">201112 season</a> in fine form, scoring the third goal in City's 40 thrashing of <a href="/wiki/Swansea_City_A.F.C." title="Swansea City A.F.C.">Swansea City</a><sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> and was voted <a href="/wiki/Man_of_the_match" class="mw-redirect" title="Man of the match">man of the match</a>. He also scored the following week against <a href="/wiki/Bolton_Wanderers_F.C." title="Bolton Wanderers F.C.">Bolton Wanderers</a>, and was again named man of the match.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> Silva then set up two of <a href="/wiki/Sergio_Ag%C3%BCero" title="Sergio Agüero">Sergio Agüero</a>'s three goals in City's second home game against Wigan Athletic. He was beginning to form a great understanding with the Argentine, with the pair having combined to score three goals already. After a series of magnificent displays from Silva, City boss Roberto Mancini compared him to fellow Spain internationals <a href="/wiki/Xavi" title="Xavi">Xavi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Andr%C3%A9s_Iniesta" title="Andrés Iniesta">Andrés Iniesta</a> and said that Silva is "one of the best players in the world."<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> On 1 October, Silva was awarded the <a href="/wiki/Premier_League_Player_of_the_Month" title="Premier League Player of the Month">Premier League Player of the Month</a> for his outstanding performances, making it the first time ever that two Manchester City players have won the award in back-to-back months with Edin Deko winning it the month before.<sup id="cite_ref-POTM1_39-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POTM1-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the first <a href="/wiki/Manchester_Derby" class="mw-redirect" title="Manchester Derby">Manchester Derby</a> of the season at <a href="/wiki/Old_Trafford" title="Old Trafford">Old Trafford</a>, Manchester City won 61, with Silva proving, yet again, to be instrumental in the Manchester City attack, scoring the fifth goal, setting up Edin Deko's second with a chested volley pass through the United defense, and participating in the first two goals with excellent passing to <a href="/wiki/James_Milner" title="James Milner">James Milner</a> to assist <a href="/wiki/Mario_Balotelli" title="Mario Balotelli">Mario Balotelli</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> He was described as having been "two steps ahead of all the United players" in the aftermath of the match.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> On 25 October 2011, in an interview with a Spanish radio station, Silva revealed that he turned down <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona" title="FC Barcelona">Barcelona</a> and <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_C.F." class="mw-redirect" title="Real Madrid C.F.">Real Madrid</a> so he could sign for City, and that he wants to stay at the club for years. He commented, "Madrid and Barcelona are great teams, but I'm happy here and I would like to stay here for many years."<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> Former City and <a href="/wiki/England_national_football_team" title="England national football team">England</a> defender <a href="/wiki/Earl_Barrett" title="Earl Barrett">Earl Barrett</a> said he is almost impossible to stop due to his ability to create space<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Andy_Cole" title="Andy Cole">Andy Cole</a>, who mostly played for Manchester United, has stated that Silva "is a joy to watch."<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Silva scored a goal in City's 32 away win against <a href="/wiki/Queens_Park_Rangers_F.C." title="Queens Park Rangers F.C.">Queens Park Rangers</a> on 5 November<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> and also scored in City's 10 home win against <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a> on 18 December.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> He also contributed by scoring the fourth goal in City's 40 win against <a href="/wiki/West_Bromwich_Albion_F.C." title="West Bromwich Albion F.C.">West Bromwich Albion</a> on 11 April 2012.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> Having done well to cut the gap between them and Manchester United to just three points, City went into April's <a href="/wiki/Manchester_derby" title="Manchester derby">Manchester Derby</a> knowing that a win would be enough to send them top of the Premier League on goal difference. In a match widely billed as the biggest game in Premier League history,<sup id="cite_ref-:4_48-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:4-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> Silva delivered a corner which was headed home by Vincent Kompany for the winner.<sup id="cite_ref-:4_48-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:4-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> City triumphed 10, and returned to the league summit having been eight points behind their city rivals as recently as the start of that month.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 13 May 2012, with City heading into the final day of the season needing a win over QPR to secure their first top flight title in 44 years, Silva delivered a cross for Edin Deko to score the equaliser in the 91st minute of the match. In addition to winning his first Premier League medal with Manchester City, he also finished the season on top of the assists table with 15 assists to his name<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> and was one of four City players who made it in the PFA's <a href="/wiki/PFA_Team_of_the_Year" title="PFA Team of the Year">Premier League Team of the Year</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-1112PFA_51-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1112PFA-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2012.E2.80.9313_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201213_season">201213 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=David_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: 201213 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:29%; ;"><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1012376600">.mw-parser-output .quotebox{background-color:#F9F9F9;border:1px solid #aaa;box-sizing:border-box;padding:10px;font-size:88%;max-width:100%}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft{margin:0.5em 1.4em 0.8em 0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright{margin:0.5em 0 0.8em 1.4em}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.centered{margin:0.5em auto 0.8em auto}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft p,.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright p{font-style:inherit}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-title{background-color:#F9F9F9;text-align:center;font-size:larger;font-weight:bold}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:before{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:"  ";vertical-align:-45%;line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:after{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:"  ";line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .left-aligned{text-align:left}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .right-aligned{text-align:right}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .center-aligned{text-align:center}.mw-parser-output .quotebox cite{display:block;font-style:normal}@media screen and (max-width:640px){.mw-parser-output .quotebox{width:100%!important;margin:0 0 0.8em!important;float:none!important}}</style>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"He is the maestro, he knows where the passes are going to go. He runs the game. A joy to watch."</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style=""><a href="/wiki/Jamie_Redknapp" title="Jamie Redknapp">Jamie Redknapp</a></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>On 17 September 2012, Silva signed a new five-year deal at City, committing himself to the Etihad Stadium until 2017.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup>
Just six days after signing his new contract, Silva got off the mark in the <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_Premier_League" title="201213 Premier League">201213 Premier League</a> season, registering an assist for <a href="/wiki/Joleon_Lescott" title="Joleon Lescott">Joleon Lescott</a> in a 11 draw with Arsenal.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> He followed this up with another assist the following week, as he played in Aguero to score against Fulham at Craven Cottage.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> He injured himself playing for Spain in October, which meant he had to miss three games for Manchester City. On 11 November, he provided the crucial assist, a lofted through-ball, to striker <a href="/wiki/Edin_D%C5%BEeko" title="Edin Deko">Edin Deko</a>, who converted in the 88th minute to steal a 21 victory over <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C." title="Tottenham Hotspur F.C.">Tottenham Hotspur</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> His first league goal of the season came in a 50 thrashing of <a href="/wiki/Aston_Villa_F.C." title="Aston Villa F.C.">Aston Villa</a> at home in the very next league match, on 17 November.
</p><p>On 19 January 2013, Silva scored twice against <a href="/wiki/Fulham_F.C." title="Fulham F.C.">Fulham</a> at home in a 20 win. On 9 March, he scored the fifth and final goal in Manchester City's 50 win against <a href="/wiki/Barnsley_F.C." title="Barnsley F.C.">Barnsley</a> at the <a href="/wiki/City_of_Manchester_Stadium" title="City of Manchester Stadium">City of Manchester Stadium</a> in the quarter-finals of the <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_FA_Cup" title="201213 FA Cup">FA Cup</a>, sealing progression to the semi-finals. In the penultimate Premier League game against <a href="/wiki/Reading_F.C." title="Reading F.C.">Reading</a>, Silva made a superb pass to Deko which took the entire Reading defense out of the game.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> Deko scored, sealing a 02 win in City's first match since the sacking of Roberto Mancini. Silva finished the season with four goals and ten assists in 32 league appearances for a City squad that finished runners-up to city rivals <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a> for the Premier League title.
</p>
<h4><span id="2013.E2.80.9314_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201314_season">201314 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=David_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: 201314 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_Premier_League" title="201314 Premier League">201314 Premier League season</a> was a tough one for Silva, as numerous injuries limited him to just 27 league appearances. Nonetheless, he did well to maintain his stellar record of goals and assists for Manchester City. On 19 August 2013, Silva scored Manchester City's opening goal of the campaign in a 40 win against <a href="/wiki/Newcastle_United_F.C." title="Newcastle United F.C.">Newcastle United</a> at the City of Manchester Stadium.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> He followed this up with an assist in the 32 defeat at Cardiff, crossing for <a href="/wiki/%C3%81lvaro_Negredo" title="Álvaro Negredo">Alvaro Negredo</a> to score.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> On 5 October, Silva began one of his most productive spells in the Premier League. Making his first league start since August following a number of injury setbacks,<sup id="cite_ref-:5_59-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:5-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> he assisted Sergio Aguero to score against <a href="/wiki/Everton_F.C." title="Everton F.C.">Everton</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> before scoring once and setting up another in a 31 victory over <a href="/wiki/West_Ham_United_F.C." title="West Ham United F.C.">West Ham</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> Silva then scored again in the 70 home win over Norwich on 2 November, but his good form was curtailed by a calf injury, which ruled him out of City's next six games.
</p><p>He made his return on 14 December, scoring at home in a 63 win over <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> before setting up goals in each of the next two games against Fulham and Liverpool. Silva was also enjoying one of his most productive <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> campaigns to date, having managed three assists and a goal in Group D, including a strike in a 32 win over champions <a href="/wiki/FC_Bayern_Munich" title="FC Bayern Munich">Bayern Munich</a><sup id="cite_ref-:5_59-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:5-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> in December.
</p><p>The month of March was a productive one for Silva, as he registered two goals and two assists in the league, along with a slew of excellent performances. He was named Manchester City's Player of the Month for March 2014, after scoring in away matches against <a href="/wiki/Hull_City_A.F.C." title="Hull City A.F.C.">Hull City</a> and <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Mar14POTM_63-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Mar14POTM-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> Silva followed this up with a goal and assist against Liverpool at <a href="/wiki/Anfield" title="Anfield">Anfield</a>, but could not prevent the Blues slipping to a 32 defeat.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> However, following a strong run of form in the final five games of the season, City pipped the Merseysiders to the title, and Silva claimed his second Premier League winners medal to add to the one from 201112. He ended the campaign with eight goals and 16 assists in all competitions.
</p>
<h4><span id="2014.E2.80.9315_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201415_season">201415 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=David_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: 201415 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:David_Silva_(14701610108).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/75/David_Silva_%2814701610108%29.jpg/220px-David_Silva_%2814701610108%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="235" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/75/David_Silva_%2814701610108%29.jpg/330px-David_Silva_%2814701610108%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/75/David_Silva_%2814701610108%29.jpg/440px-David_Silva_%2814701610108%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2180" data-file-height="2332" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:David_Silva_(14701610108).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Silva playing in the 2014 FA Community Shield against Arsenal</div></div></div>
<p>On 10 August, Silva played in the <a href="/wiki/2014_FA_Community_Shield" title="2014 FA Community Shield">2014 FA Community Shield</a>, a match City lost 30 to <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> Two days later, he signed a five-year contract extension with City.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> Like the previous season, on 17 August, Silva scored Manchester City's opening goal of the <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_Premier_League" title="201415 Premier League">201415 Premier League</a> season in a 20 away win against Newcastle United. Silva then scored against West Brom on Boxing Day.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 21 February 2015, Silva scored a brace against Newcastle United in a 50 win.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup> He won the Etihad Player of the Month award for his performances in February.<sup id="cite_ref-Feb15POTM_69-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Feb15POTM-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> On 4 March, Silva scored in 10 win against <a href="/wiki/Leicester_City_F.C." title="Leicester City F.C.">Leicester City</a> to take him to ten league goals in a season for the first time in his career.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Jamie_Redknapp" title="Jamie Redknapp">Jamie Redknapp</a> described him as a "maestro" for his performances for City,<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup> while his teammate Edin Deko called him "the best player in the Premier League."<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 19 April, in a 20 victory over West Ham, Silva was caught in the face by the elbow of <a href="/wiki/Cheikhou_Kouyat%C3%A9" title="Cheikhou Kouyaté">Cheikhou Kouyaté</a>, requiring eight minutes of treatment before being substituted for <a href="/wiki/Samir_Nasri" title="Samir Nasri">Samir Nasri</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup> Tests confirmed that he had not fractured his cheekbone.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup> On 10 May, Silva scored a goal in City's 60 win over Queens Park Rangers, which resulted in the latter's relegation.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2015.E2.80.9316_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201516_season">201516 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=David_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: 201516 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>In the opening match of the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_Premier_League" title="201516 Premier League">Premier League</a> season, in a 03 win at <a href="/wiki/West_Bromich_Albion_F.C." class="mw-redirect" title="West Bromich Albion F.C.">West Brom</a>, Silva delivered a performance his manager <a href="/wiki/Manuel_Pellegrini" title="Manuel Pellegrini">Manuel Pellegrini</a> labelled "unbelievable".<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup> As well as assisting the team's third goal, Silva was later credited with the first goal.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> After contributing another three assists for the team in August (in wins against <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a> and <a href="/wiki/Watford_F.C." title="Watford F.C.">Watford</a>),<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup> Silva was nominated for both of the <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City_F.C." title="Manchester City F.C.">Manchester City</a> and <a href="/wiki/Premier_League_Player_of_the_Month" title="Premier League Player of the Month">Premier League Player of the Month</a> Awards for August, winning the former.<sup id="cite_ref-Aug15POTM_84-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Aug15POTM-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Silva was injured for most of October and November after picking up an ankle injury, while playing for <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_football_team" title="Spain national football team">Spain</a> on 9 October.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup> He made his return, as a 75th-minute substitute, in a 31 league defeat of <a href="/wiki/Southampton_F.C." title="Southampton F.C.">Southampton</a> on 28 November.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup> He netted the opener in the last <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_UEFA_Champions_League" title="201516 UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> group stage match on 8 December, in a 42 home defeat of <a href="/wiki/Borussia_M%C3%B6nchengladbach" title="Borussia Mönchengladbach">Borussia Mönchengladbach</a>, which resulted in Manchester City topping their group for the first time.<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup> Silva provided another three assists in home victories against <a href="/wiki/Tyne%E2%80%93Wear_derby" title="TyneWear derby">Tyne-Wear</a> rivals <a href="/wiki/Newcastle_United_F.C." title="Newcastle United F.C.">Newcastle United</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sunderland_F.C." class="mw-redirect" title="Sunderland F.C.">Sunderland</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:David_Silva_shaved_Man_City_2017_(36471171422)_(cropped).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/22/David_Silva_shaved_Man_City_2017_%2836471171422%29_%28cropped%29.jpg/170px-David_Silva_shaved_Man_City_2017_%2836471171422%29_%28cropped%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="256" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/22/David_Silva_shaved_Man_City_2017_%2836471171422%29_%28cropped%29.jpg/255px-David_Silva_shaved_Man_City_2017_%2836471171422%29_%28cropped%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/22/David_Silva_shaved_Man_City_2017_%2836471171422%29_%28cropped%29.jpg/340px-David_Silva_shaved_Man_City_2017_%2836471171422%29_%28cropped%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1145" data-file-height="1724" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:David_Silva_shaved_Man_City_2017_(36471171422)_(cropped).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Silva warming up before a preseason match against Tottenham in July 2017</div></div></div>
<p>In a 40 home league win against <a href="/wiki/Crystal_Palace_F.C." title="Crystal Palace F.C.">Crystal Palace</a> on 16 January 2016, Silva scored one, set-up another two goals and played a key pass in the remaining goal.<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup> Silva started the <a href="/wiki/2016_Football_League_Cup_Final" title="2016 Football League Cup Final">2016 Football League Cup Final</a> on 28 February, as <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City_F.C." title="Manchester City F.C.">Manchester City</a> defeated <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_F.C." title="Liverpool F.C.">Liverpool</a> 31 on penalties, winning his second League Cup with the club.<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup> He claimed another brace of assists in a 40 home defeat of <a href="/wiki/Aston_Villa_F.C." title="Aston Villa F.C.">Aston Villa</a> six days later.<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After scoring 8 goals in 44 appearances and providing numerous assists, Silva won his first <a href="/wiki/Etihad" class="mw-redirect" title="Etihad">Etihad</a> Player of the Season award for his outstanding contribution, as voted for by <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City" class="mw-redirect" title="Manchester City">Manchester City</a> fans.<sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2016.E2.80.9317_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201617_season">201617 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=David_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: 201617 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>With <a href="/wiki/Pep_Guardiola" title="Pep Guardiola">Pep Guardiola</a> arriving as Manchester City's new manager to much fanfare, it was the beginning of a new era for City. Having put pen to paper on a three-year contract with the Blues,<sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup> the legendary manager stated that one of the reasons he had come to the club was to work with Silva, whom he described as a special player, and one of the best he had ever trained.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup> In Guardiola's first season at the club, Silva scored one goal in a 50 win over <a href="/wiki/FCSB" title="FCSB">Steaua Bucureti</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_UEFA_Champions_League_qualifying_phase_and_play-off_round" title="201617 UEFA Champions League qualifying phase and play-off round">201617 UEFA Champions League play-off round</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup> He later scored the equalising goal in a 11 draw against <a href="/wiki/Borussia_M%C3%B6nchengladbach" title="Borussia Mönchengladbach">Borussia Mönchengladbach</a> in the group stage.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup> However, Manchester City finished third in the league, and they were knocked out by <a href="/wiki/AS_Monaco_FC" title="AS Monaco FC">Monaco</a> in the Champions League round of 16.<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup> He ended the campaign with 8 goals and 11 assists in all competitions, and was named Manchester City's Player of the Season.
</p>
<h4><span id="2017.E2.80.9318_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201718_season">201718 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=David_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: 201718 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Silva started the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_Manchester_City_F.C._season" title="201718 Manchester City F.C. season">201718 season</a> with yet another display of finesse, providing eight Premier League assists in 14 appearances, which was the highest total for any player in Europe's top five leagues.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup> The 201718 season was an especially difficult time for the Spaniard, with his newborn son having been born extremely prematurely. This led to him having to jet back and forth between England and Spain to visit his son and partner in a hospital in Madrid.<sup id="cite_ref-:7_103-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:7-103">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup> Despite this, Silva continued to produce excellent performances, and on 30 November 2017, he signed a one-year contract extension with Manchester City keeping him at the club until 2020.<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup> On 10 December, Silva scored the winner in a closely fought Manchester Derby at <a href="/wiki/Old_Trafford" title="Old Trafford">Old Trafford</a>, stabbing the ball past <a href="/wiki/David_de_Gea" title="David de Gea">David de Gea</a> from close range.<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Silva was forced to miss a crucial game against <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C." title="Tottenham Hotspur F.C.">Tottenham Hotspur</a> at the <a href="/wiki/City_of_Manchester_Stadium" title="City of Manchester Stadium">Etihad Stadium</a> in December, as he was with his son in Spain.<sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup> In his absence, City delivered a sumptuous performance, smashing Tottenham 41 following an urging from manager <a href="/wiki/Pep_Guardiola" title="Pep Guardiola">Pep Guardiola</a> to secure the win for Silva and his partner Yessica.<sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup> Midfielder <a href="/wiki/Kevin_De_Bruyne" title="Kevin De Bruyne">Kevin De Bruyne</a> held his fingers up to show the number 21, Silva's shirt number, after scoring City's second, in a touching tribute to the Spaniard.<sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He also scored in the <a href="/wiki/2018_EFL_Cup_Final" title="2018 EFL Cup Final">2018 EFL Cup Final</a> against <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a><sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup> For his contributions, Silva was nominated for the <a href="/wiki/PFA_Players%27_Player_of_the_Year" title="PFA Players&#39; Player of the Year">PFA Player of the Year</a> and named in the <a href="/wiki/PFA_Team_of_the_Year" title="PFA Team of the Year">PFA Team of the Year</a> for the second time as City won the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_Premier_League" title="201718 Premier League">Premier League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup> It was the third Premier League title of Silva's career, and he finished the season with 10 goals and 14 assists across all competitions.<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2018.E2.80.9319_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201819_season">201819 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=David_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: 201819 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 15 September 2018, in a 30 home win over Fulham, Silva scored his 50th Premier League goal in his 253rd appearance in the competition, also making his 350th appearance for Manchester City in the same match.<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">&#91;114&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">&#91;115&#93;</a></sup> City and Liverpool went head to head in an absorbing title race, which ended up with City pipping the Reds to the title by a single point.<sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>It was a remarkable season for the Blues, as they went on to win the <a href="/wiki/FA_Community_Shield" title="FA Community Shield">Community Shield</a>, <a href="/wiki/EFL_Cup" title="EFL Cup">League Cup</a> and <a href="/wiki/FA_Cup" title="FA Cup">FA Cup</a> too, with Silva scoring in the final of the latter tournament.<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">&#91;117&#93;</a></sup> In doing this, they became the first club in English football history to win all four domestic honours in a single season.<sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118">&#91;118&#93;</a></sup> Silva played in 33 of City's 38 league games, registering 10 goals and 14 assists in all competitions<sup id="cite_ref-119" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-119">&#91;119&#93;</a></sup> as he picked up his second FA Cup, fourth League Cup and fourth Premier League title.
</p>
<h4><span id="2019.E2.80.9320_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201920_season">201920 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=David_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: 201920 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Following the departure of <a href="/wiki/Vincent_Kompany" title="Vincent Kompany">Vincent Kompany</a> in 2019, Silva inherited the club <a href="/wiki/Captain_(association_football)" title="Captain (association football)">captaincy</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120">&#91;120&#93;</a></sup> On 26 June 2019, Silva announced that he would leave Manchester City at the end of the <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_Manchester_City_F.C._season" title="201920 Manchester City F.C. season">201920 season</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-:0_14-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> The campaign began with City facing Liverpool in the Community Shield at Wembley- City won on penalties following a 1-1 draw,<sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121">&#91;121&#93;</a></sup> with Silva producing a brilliant pass to assist <a href="/wiki/Raheem_Sterling" title="Raheem Sterling">Raheem Sterling</a> for City's goal. On 8 July, he provided two assists, the second of which was his 10th of the season, and scored a free kick as City beat Newcastle United 50. With the free kick goal, he reached 150 Premier League goals and assists, which only a few midfielders had done before.<sup id="cite_ref-122" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-122">&#91;122&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-123" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-123">&#91;123&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 1 March 2020, City took on <a href="/wiki/Aston_Villa_F.C." title="Aston Villa F.C.">Aston Villa</a> in the League Cup final,<sup id="cite_ref-124" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-124">&#91;124&#93;</a></sup> their third such final in as many years and fifth in seven seasons. The Blues won 2-1, with goals from Sergio Aguero and <a href="/wiki/Rodri_(footballer,_born_1996)" title="Rodri (footballer, born 1996)">Rodri</a>, and lifted the trophy for the third time in a row. It was Silva's only trophy as captain of Manchester City, and his fifth League Cup title overall, making him the most decorated player in the competition's 60-year history.<sup id="cite_ref-125" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-125">&#91;125&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 26 July 2020, Silva played his final Premier League game for Manchester City, a 50 win over <a href="/wiki/Norwich_City_F.C." title="Norwich City F.C.">Norwich City</a>. He was substituted late on in the match, to applause from all present.<sup id="cite_ref-126" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-126">&#91;126&#93;</a></sup> Just under a month later, he played his last game in a City shirt, in a disappointing 31 defeat to <a href="/wiki/Olympique_Lyonnais" title="Olympique Lyonnais">Olympique Lyon</a> in the Champions League quarter-finals, coming on as a late substitute.<sup id="cite_ref-127" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-127">&#91;127&#93;</a></sup> At the age of 34, Silva ended the campaign with a respectable return of six goals and 11 assists in all competitions, enough to earn himself a third appearance in the <a href="/wiki/PFA_Team_of_the_Year" title="PFA Team of the Year">PFA Team of the Year</a> despite City's underwhelming season.<sup id="cite_ref-128" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-128">&#91;128&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Club chairman <a href="/wiki/Khaldoon_Al_Mubarak" title="Khaldoon Al Mubarak">Khaldoon Al Mubarak</a> announced plans for a statue of Silva, along with teammates Sergio Aguero and Vincent Kompany, to be installed at the Etihad Stadium to commemorate his 10-year "transformational" contribution at City.<sup id="cite_ref-129" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-129">&#91;129&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Real_Sociedad">Real Sociedad</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=David_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Real Sociedad">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>On 17 August 2020, Spanish club <a href="/wiki/Real_Sociedad" title="Real Sociedad">Real Sociedad</a> announced the signing of Silva on a free transfer,<sup id="cite_ref-130" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-130">&#91;130&#93;</a></sup> despite reports of a move to Italian side <a href="/wiki/S.S._Lazio" title="S.S. Lazio">Lazio</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-131" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-131">&#91;131&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Silva made his debut for the club in a 00 home draw against <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_CF" title="Real Madrid CF">Real Madrid</a>, coming on as a substitute in the second half.<sup id="cite_ref-132" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-132">&#91;132&#93;</a></sup> On 25 October 2020, Silva provided two assists as La Real beat <a href="/wiki/SD_Huesca" title="SD Huesca">Huesca</a> 4-1 in La Liga.<sup id="cite_ref-133" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-133">&#91;133&#93;</a></sup> A week later, he scored his first goal for the club, in a 41 away win against <a href="/wiki/RC_Celta_de_Vigo" title="RC Celta de Vigo">Celta Vigo</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134">&#91;134&#93;</a></sup> Following his excellent performances for Sociedad, Silva was named in WhoScored's La Liga Team of the Month for November,<sup id="cite_ref-135" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-135">&#91;135&#93;</a></sup> as well as being named Real Sociedad Player of the Month.<sup id="cite_ref-:6_136-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:6-136">&#91;136&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 21 February 2021, Silva once again provided two assists as Real Sociedad defeated <a href="/wiki/Deportivo_Alav%C3%A9s" title="Deportivo Alavés">Alaves</a> 4-0 in the league.<sup id="cite_ref-137" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-137">&#91;137&#93;</a></sup> This propelled La Real to 5th in the table, while Silva became the only player to provide two assists in two different La Liga games that season.<sup id="cite_ref-138" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-138">&#91;138&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_career">International career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=David_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: International career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;"><a href="/wiki/File:David_Silva_2018.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b8/David_Silva_2018.jpg/150px-David_Silva_2018.jpg" decoding="async" width="150" height="164" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b8/David_Silva_2018.jpg/225px-David_Silva_2018.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b8/David_Silva_2018.jpg/300px-David_Silva_2018.jpg 2x" data-file-width="732" data-file-height="800" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:David_Silva_2018.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Silva representing <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_football_team" title="Spain national football team">Spain</a> at the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a> in Russia.</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Leonardo_Bonucci_and_David_Silva_Euro_2012_final_02.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a0/Leonardo_Bonucci_and_David_Silva_Euro_2012_final_02.jpg/200px-Leonardo_Bonucci_and_David_Silva_Euro_2012_final_02.jpg" decoding="async" width="200" height="169" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a0/Leonardo_Bonucci_and_David_Silva_Euro_2012_final_02.jpg/300px-Leonardo_Bonucci_and_David_Silva_Euro_2012_final_02.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a0/Leonardo_Bonucci_and_David_Silva_Euro_2012_final_02.jpg/400px-Leonardo_Bonucci_and_David_Silva_Euro_2012_final_02.jpg 2x" data-file-width="656" data-file-height="553" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Leonardo_Bonucci_and_David_Silva_Euro_2012_final_02.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Silva being pressured by Italian defender <a href="/wiki/Leonardo_Bonucci" title="Leonardo Bonucci">Leonardo Bonucci</a> in the UEFA Euro 2012 Final.</div></div></div>
<p>Silva first represented Spain in the <a href="/wiki/2003_FIFA_U-17_World_Championship" title="2003 FIFA U-17 World Championship">2003 FIFA U-17 World Championship</a> in <a href="/wiki/Finland" title="Finland">Finland</a>, scoring three goals. In 2006, he became an <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_under-21_football_team" title="Spain national under-21 football team">under-21 international</a> and scored four goals during the <a href="/wiki/2005_FIFA_World_Youth_Championship" title="2005 FIFA World Youth Championship">2005 FIFA World Youth Championship</a>; this was enough to earn him joint-fourth place in the goal ranking, alongside Italian <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)" title="Forward (association football)">striker</a> <a href="/wiki/Graziano_Pell%C3%A8" title="Graziano Pellè">Graziano Pellè</a>.
</p><p>Silva made his <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_football_team" title="Spain national football team">senior international</a> debut in the 10 friendly home defeat to <a href="/wiki/Romania_national_football_team" title="Romania national football team">Romania</a> on 15 November 2006, and continued to receive call-ups to the side after good contributions in his first games. On 22 August 2007, he scored his first two goals for Spain, netting twice in a 32 friendly win versus <a href="/wiki/Greece_national_football_team" title="Greece national football team">Greece</a>, and was then called up to the squad of 23 for <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2008" title="UEFA Euro 2008">UEFA Euro 2008</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="UEFA_Euro_2008">UEFA Euro 2008</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=David_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: UEFA Euro 2008">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Silva started five of Spain's six matches at Euro 2008. In Spain's second group stage match against Sweden in Innsbruck, he assisted <a href="/wiki/Fernando_Torres" title="Fernando Torres">Fernando Torres</a> with a pinpoint cross from the edge of the box,<sup id="cite_ref-139" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-139">&#91;139&#93;</a></sup> with the <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_F.C." title="Liverpool F.C.">Liverpool</a> forward scoring the opener in an eventual 21 win.
</p><p>In the semi-finals game versus <a href="/wiki/Russia_national_football_team" title="Russia national football team">Russia</a>, Silva scored the third goal for Spain after a quick counter-attack in which <a href="/wiki/Cesc_F%C3%A0bregas" title="Cesc Fàbregas">Cesc Fàbregas</a> delivered a low cross, and he sent the ball into <a href="/wiki/Igor_Akinfeev" title="Igor Akinfeev">Igor Akinfeev</a>'s goal with his left foot.<sup id="cite_ref-140" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-140">&#91;140&#93;</a></sup> In <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2008_Final" title="UEFA Euro 2008 Final">the final</a>, he was involved in an incident with <a href="/wiki/Germany_national_football_team" title="Germany national football team">Germany</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Lukas_Podolski" title="Lukas Podolski">Lukas Podolski</a>. After he pulled Podolski to the ground, the German approached Silva, which resulted in an angry exchange of words and a coming together of heads that the referee decided not to punish. Shortly afterward, Spanish coach <a href="/wiki/Luis_Aragon%C3%A9s" title="Luis Aragonés">Luis Aragonés</a> substituted Silva for <a href="/wiki/Santi_Cazorla" title="Santi Cazorla">Santi Cazorla</a> in an attempt to calm the tensions.<sup id="cite_ref-141" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-141">&#91;141&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2010_FIFA_World_Cup">2010 FIFA World Cup</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=David_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: 2010 FIFA World Cup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>After appearing regularly during <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2010 FIFA World Cup">2010 FIFA World Cup</a> <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_(UEFA)" title="2010 FIFA World Cup qualification (UEFA)">qualification</a>  Spain won all ten fixtures  Silva was also picked for the squad for the finals in <a href="/wiki/South_Africa" title="South Africa">South Africa</a>. His participation was, however, a small one. He started the opening group game for La Furia Roja, against Switzerland in Durban, but despite some bright sparks, the European champions succumbed to a 10 defeat.<sup id="cite_ref-142" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-142">&#91;142&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Silva next appeared for Spain in the semi-final against Germany, replacing <a href="/wiki/Pedro_(footballer,_born_1987)" title="Pedro (footballer, born 1987)">Pedro</a> for the final nine minutes.<sup id="cite_ref-143" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-143">&#91;143&#93;</a></sup> Spain won 10, courtesy of a header from <a href="/wiki/Carles_Puyol" title="Carles Puyol">Carles Puyol</a>, and went on to win the tournament, beating the <a href="/wiki/Netherlands_national_football_team" title="Netherlands national football team">Netherlands</a> in the final.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="UEFA_Euro_2012_Qualifying">UEFA Euro 2012 Qualifying</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=David_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: UEFA Euro 2012 Qualifying">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3><p>
On 11 August 2010, during an international friendly with <a href="/wiki/Mexico_national_football_team" title="Mexico national football team">Mexico</a>, Silva scored two minutes into second-half injury time, ending the game with a 11 draw.<sup id="cite_ref-144" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-144">&#91;144&#93;</a></sup> In a <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012_qualifying" title="UEFA Euro 2012 qualifying">Euro 2012 qualifier</a> against <a href="/wiki/Liechtenstein_national_football_team" title="Liechtenstein national football team">Liechtenstein</a> on 3 September 2010, Silva scored after 62 minutes, in a 40 away win.<sup id="cite_ref-145" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-145">&#91;145&#93;</a></sup> The following month, in the same competition, he scored through a rare header, as the national team downed <a href="/wiki/Lithuania_national_football_team" title="Lithuania national football team">Lithuania</a> in <a href="/wiki/Salamanca" title="Salamanca">Salamanca</a> (31).</p><div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:David_Silva_and_Leonardo_Bonucci_Euro_2012_final.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cb/David_Silva_and_Leonardo_Bonucci_Euro_2012_final.jpg/220px-David_Silva_and_Leonardo_Bonucci_Euro_2012_final.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="155" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cb/David_Silva_and_Leonardo_Bonucci_Euro_2012_final.jpg/330px-David_Silva_and_Leonardo_Bonucci_Euro_2012_final.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cb/David_Silva_and_Leonardo_Bonucci_Euro_2012_final.jpg/440px-David_Silva_and_Leonardo_Bonucci_Euro_2012_final.jpg 2x" data-file-width="656" data-file-height="462" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:David_Silva_and_Leonardo_Bonucci_Euro_2012_final.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Silva (left) on the ball for Spain in the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012_Final" title="UEFA Euro 2012 Final">UEFA Euro 2012 Final</a></div></div></div><p>In a friendly against <a href="/wiki/Colombia_national_football_team" title="Colombia national football team">Colombia</a> on 9 February 2011, he came off the bench to score the game's only goal with just four minutes remaining, helping Spain to a hard-fought 10 win.<sup id="cite_ref-146" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-146">&#91;146&#93;</a></sup> He scored twice and provided one assist in Spain's 31 victory against <a href="/wiki/Scotland_national_football_team" title="Scotland national football team">Scotland</a> in their final match of the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012_qualifying" title="UEFA Euro 2012 qualifying">Euro 2012 qualifiers</a>. The win saw the Spaniards enter the tournament with a perfect qualifying record by winning all their group games.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> He scored the first goal in Spain's 22 comeback against <a href="/wiki/Costa_Rica_national_football_team" title="Costa Rica national football team">Costa Rica</a>, a friendly match where he came on as a substitute in the second half with Spain trailing 20.<sup id="cite_ref-147" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-147">&#91;147&#93;</a></sup> He once again scored in a friendly against <a href="/wiki/Venezuela_national_football_team" title="Venezuela national football team">Venezuela</a> to make the score 20 in a match that ended in a 50 win. Heading into Euro 2012, he scored in their pre-tournament friendly against <a href="/wiki/China_football_team" class="mw-redirect" title="China football team">China</a> by finishing off a short give and go from <a href="/wiki/Andr%C3%A9s_Iniesta" title="Andrés Iniesta">Andrés Iniesta</a> in the 84th minute.
</p><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="UEFA_Euro_2012">UEFA Euro 2012</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=David_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: UEFA Euro 2012">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Silva was a starter in all six matches of Spain's Euro 2012 campaign. In their opening match of the tournament against <a href="/wiki/Italy_national_football_team" title="Italy national football team">Italy</a>, he delivered a superb flicked through ball to Cesc Fabregas,<sup id="cite_ref-148" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-148">&#91;148&#93;</a></sup> who scored to level the game up at 11.
</p><p>In Spain's second Group C match against the Republic of Ireland, Silva produced one of the performances of the tournament, scoring one and providing two assists in a 40 win.<sup id="cite_ref-149" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-149">&#91;149&#93;</a></sup> His goal was mesmeric, as he left <a href="/wiki/Sean_St_Ledger" title="Sean St Ledger">Sean St. Ledger</a> on the floor and beat <a href="/wiki/Stephen_Ward_(footballer)" title="Stephen Ward (footballer)">Stephen Ward</a> before coolly slotting it past former Manchester City teammate <a href="/wiki/Shay_Given" title="Shay Given">Shay Given</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-150" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-150">&#91;150&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the 14th minute of the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012_Final" title="UEFA Euro 2012 Final">UEFA Euro 2012 Final</a>, he headed home a Cesc Fàbregas cross, giving Spain a 10 lead.<sup id="cite_ref-151" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-151">&#91;151&#93;</a></sup>
The match ended 40 and concluded the tournament in which Silva scored two goals and made three assists, the best efficiency (goals and assists) of any player at the Euros.<sup id="cite_ref-:1_152-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:1-152">&#91;152&#93;</a></sup> He was subsequently named in UEFA's Euro 2012 Team of the Tournament for his performances.<sup id="cite_ref-153" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-153">&#91;153&#93;</a></sup> He also finished as the joint highest assist provider at the Euros, with three.<sup id="cite_ref-:2_154-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:2-154">&#91;154&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2013_FIFA_Confederations_Cup">2013 FIFA Confederations Cup</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=David_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: 2013 FIFA Confederations Cup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Silva was named in Vicente del Bosque's 23-man squad list for Spain's contestation of the <a href="/wiki/2013_FIFA_Confederations_Cup" title="2013 FIFA Confederations Cup">2013 FIFA Confederations Cup</a>, held in Brazil. On 20 June 2013, he scored two goals and assisted one for David Villa in Spain's 100 <a href="/wiki/2013_FIFA_Confederations_Cup_Group_B" title="2013 FIFA Confederations Cup Group B">group stage</a> demolition of <a href="/wiki/Tahiti_national_football_team" title="Tahiti national football team">Tahiti</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Maracan%C3%A3_Stadium" title="Maracanã Stadium">Maracanã</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-155" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-155">&#91;155&#93;</a></sup> Spain would go on to reach the <a href="/wiki/2013_FIFA_Confederations_Cup_Final" title="2013 FIFA Confederations Cup Final">2013 FIFA Confederations Cup Final</a>, where they were soundly beaten 30 by hosts Brazil.<sup id="cite_ref-156" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-156">&#91;156&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2014_FIFA_World_Cup">2014 FIFA World Cup</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=David_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: 2014 FIFA World Cup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Silva was part of Spain's 23-man squad which traveled to Brazil for the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 World Cup</a>. With La Roja looking to defend the title they captured four years ago in South Africa, Silva started the opening match against the <a href="/wiki/Netherlands_national_football_team" title="Netherlands national football team">Netherlands</a> in Bahia. However, they were unable to repeat their success over the Oranje from 2010, and succumbed to a 5-1 loss, despite taking an early lead.<sup id="cite_ref-157" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-157">&#91;157&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Silva started the second group stage game, against <a href="/wiki/Chile_national_football_team" title="Chile national football team">Chile</a>, playing the full 90 minutes.<sup id="cite_ref-158" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-158">&#91;158&#93;</a></sup> However, it was another bad outing for the side, who were soundly beaten 2-0 and eliminated from the tournament.<sup id="cite_ref-159" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-159">&#91;159&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Despite the team's under-performance, Silva was one of the brighter sparks for La Roja, creating seven chances for his team, the most of any Spanish player at the World Cup.<sup id="cite_ref-160" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-160">&#91;160&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="UEFA_Euro_2016">UEFA Euro 2016</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=David_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: UEFA Euro 2016">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
