<p><a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016" title="UEFA Euro 2016">Euro 2016</a> was one of Silva's best outings for the National Team at a major tournament. Starting in all four matches, Silva began the tournament with a show stopping display against the <a href="/wiki/Czech_Republic_national_football_team" title="Czech Republic national football team">Czech Republic</a>, in which he created six chances for his team- the most of any Spain player in a single match at the tournament.<sup id="cite_ref-161" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-161">&#91;161&#93;</a></sup> The game ended in  a 1-0 victory for the reigning European champions.<sup id="cite_ref-162" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-162">&#91;162&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the second group game, a clash with <a href="/wiki/Turkey_national_football_team" title="Turkey national football team">Turkey</a> in Nice, Silva was a key cog as Spain produced one of their best performances of the tournament, dispatching the Turks 3-0.<sup id="cite_ref-163" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-163">&#91;163&#93;</a></sup> Silva was mesmeric throughout, and received a standing ovation from Spain and Turkey fans alike when he was substituted late in the game.
</p><p>Silva played the full 90 minutes in La Roja's third group stage game against <a href="/wiki/Croatia_national_football_team" title="Croatia national football team">Croatia</a>. It was an exceptional display, with the midfielder playing a sublime through ball to teammate Cesc Fabregas, who squared for <a href="/wiki/%C3%81lvaro_Morata" title="Álvaro Morata">Alvaro Morata</a> to score the opener. He later won a penalty, which was missed by <a href="/wiki/Sergio_Ramos" title="Sergio Ramos">Sergio Ramos</a>, as Spain fell to a 2-1 defeat.<sup id="cite_ref-164" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-164">&#91;164&#93;</a></sup> Despite this, Silva created five chances in the game, the second most of any Spain player in a Euro 2016 match, after himself.<sup id="cite_ref-165" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-165">&#91;165&#93;</a></sup> Spain were eventually eliminated in the quarter-final by <a href="/wiki/Italy_national_football_team" title="Italy national football team">Italy</a>, who beat them 2-0.<sup id="cite_ref-166" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-166">&#91;166&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Silva ended the tournament averaging 3.3 chances created per 90, the third highest at the tournament.<sup id="cite_ref-167" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-167">&#91;167&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Later_years_and_retirement">Later years and retirement</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=David_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Later years and retirement">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Silva continued his goal scoring record under new boss Julen Lopetegui, scoring 9 times in 12 matches.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2017)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> In May 2018, Silva was named to Spain's squad for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a> in Russia.<sup id="cite_ref-168" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-168">&#91;168&#93;</a></sup> He started all their matches in their World Cup campaign, which eventually ended with a 34 penalty shootout defeat to hosts Russia in the Round of 16.
</p><p>After the 2018 World Cup, Silva announced his retirement from international football.<sup id="cite_ref-169" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-169">&#91;169&#93;</a></sup> He ended his international career with 125 caps for Spain, having scored 35 goals. Following his retirement, Silva drew plaudits from many of his former teammates, being described as "one of the best ever"<sup id="cite_ref-:3_170-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:3-170">&#91;170&#93;</a></sup> and "one of the most talented players Spain has ever produced, without a shadow of a doubt"<sup id="cite_ref-:3_170-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:3-170">&#91;170&#93;</a></sup> by midfield partners Andres Iniesta and Xavi Hernandez. Vicente del Bosque, who led Spain to the 2010 World Cup and Euro 2012 titles, even went as far as to declare Silva "Spain's Lionel Messi".<sup id="cite_ref-171" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-171">&#91;171&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Style_of_play">Style of play</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=David_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Style of play">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:29%; ;"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1012376600"/>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"He pulls the strings on the pitch. A brilliant footballer with great movement, he can score, assist, a player who decides a game. Hes got so much to his game, that I would consider him one of the best ever."</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style=""><a href="/wiki/Andr%C3%A9s_Iniesta" title="Andrés Iniesta">Andrés Iniesta</a><sup id="cite_ref-iniestaquote_172-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-iniestaquote-172">&#91;172&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:29%; ;"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1012376600"/>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"Hes a spectacular footballer. He has been throughout his career. For the national team he has been a cornerstone of that generation of highly talented Spanish footballers. David was a vital component and absolutely essential to that team - one of the most talented players Spain has ever produced, without a shadow of a doubt."<sup id="cite_ref-iniestaquote_172-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-iniestaquote-172">&#91;172&#93;</a></sup></div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style=""><a href="/wiki/Xavi" title="Xavi">Xavi</a></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>A talented and agile left-footed player,<sup id="cite_ref-How_Pellegrini_will_seek_to_get_the_best_out_of_City&#39;s_wide_men_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-How_Pellegrini_will_seek_to_get_the_best_out_of_City&#39;s_wide_men-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-173" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-173">&#91;173&#93;</a></sup> Silva is known for having an excellent first touch, good <a href="/wiki/Dribbling" title="Dribbling">dribbling</a> skills, and outstanding technical ability, which, along with his intelligent attacking movements, allow him to retain possession in tight spaces, and to create space for himself and teammates to open up a defence.<sup id="cite_ref-Play_without_a_striker_174-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Play_without_a_striker-174">&#91;174&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-David_Silva_as_good_as_Eden_Hazard_and_Arjen_Robben_175-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-David_Silva_as_good_as_Eden_Hazard_and_Arjen_Robben-175">&#91;175&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-David_Silva_the_shining_light_as_Manchester_City_escape_United_shadow_176-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-David_Silva_the_shining_light_as_Manchester_City_escape_United_shadow-176">&#91;176&#93;</a></sup> His composure on the ball, as well as his vision, passing accuracy, ability to read the game, pick a pass, and control the tempo of his team's play have seen him become one of the best players in the world in his position, as well as one of the best midfielders in Premier League history, and earned him the nicknames <i><a href="/wiki/Merlin" title="Merlin">Merlin</a></i> and <i>El Mago</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-How_Pellegrini_will_seek_to_get_the_best_out_of_City&#39;s_wide_men_3-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-How_Pellegrini_will_seek_to_get_the_best_out_of_City&#39;s_wide_men-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-David_Silva,_or_is_it_Merlin?_4-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-David_Silva,_or_is_it_Merlin?-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-HBD_Merlin_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBD_Merlin-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Premier_Leagues_best_ever_midfielders_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Premier_Leagues_best_ever_midfielders-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-David_Silva_as_good_as_Eden_Hazard_and_Arjen_Robben_175-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-David_Silva_as_good_as_Eden_Hazard_and_Arjen_Robben-175">&#91;175&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-David_Silva_the_shining_light_as_Manchester_City_escape_United_shadow_176-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-David_Silva_the_shining_light_as_Manchester_City_escape_United_shadow-176">&#91;176&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Man_City_want_Silva_and_Aguero_back_as_soon_as_possible_177-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Man_City_want_Silva_and_Aguero_back_as_soon_as_possible-177">&#91;177&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-178" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-178">&#91;178&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-179" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-179">&#91;179&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Although he primarily serves as a <a href="/wiki/Playmaker" title="Playmaker">playmaker</a> for his team,<sup id="cite_ref-Man_City_want_Silva_and_Aguero_back_as_soon_as_possible_177-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Man_City_want_Silva_and_Aguero_back_as_soon_as_possible-177">&#91;177&#93;</a></sup> he is capable of scoring goals himself as well as creating them,<sup id="cite_ref-David_Silva_as_good_as_Eden_Hazard_and_Arjen_Robben_175-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-David_Silva_as_good_as_Eden_Hazard_and_Arjen_Robben-175">&#91;175&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-180" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-180">&#91;180&#93;</a></sup> which enables him to be deployed in several offensive roles:<sup id="cite_ref-How_Pellegrini_will_seek_to_get_the_best_out_of_City&#39;s_wide_men_3-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-How_Pellegrini_will_seek_to_get_the_best_out_of_City&#39;s_wide_men-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Play_without_a_striker_174-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Play_without_a_striker-174">&#91;174&#93;</a></sup> he is usually fielded in a free role as an <a href="/wiki/Attacking_midfielder" class="mw-redirect" title="Attacking midfielder">attacking midfielder</a>, where he is given space to roam the pitch,<sup id="cite_ref-181" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-181">&#91;181&#93;</a></sup> but has also been used as a <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#Winger" title="Forward (association football)">winger</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-182" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-182">&#91;182&#93;</a></sup> as a <a href="/wiki/False_9" class="mw-redirect" title="False 9">false 9</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-Play_without_a_striker_174-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Play_without_a_striker-174">&#91;174&#93;</a></sup> as a <a href="/wiki/Second_striker" class="mw-redirect" title="Second striker">second striker</a> or as a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Deep-lying_playmaker" title="Midfielder">deeper-lying</a> <a href="/wiki/Central_midfielder" class="mw-redirect" title="Central midfielder">central midfielder</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-How_Pellegrini_will_seek_to_get_the_best_out_of_City&#39;s_wide_men_3-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-How_Pellegrini_will_seek_to_get_the_best_out_of_City&#39;s_wide_men-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Play_without_a_striker_174-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Play_without_a_striker-174">&#91;174&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-183" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-183">&#91;183&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=David_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Personal life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>During December 2017, Silva had been missing games to return to Spain for personal reasons. On 3 January 2018, he said that his new son, Mateo, had been born extremely prematurely and was fighting to stay alive.<sup id="cite_ref-:7_103-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:7-103">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup> On 11 May 2018, Mateo was reported as healthy and was allowed to come home.<sup id="cite_ref-184" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-184">&#91;184&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 31 August 2020, he tested positive for <a href="/wiki/COVID-19" title="COVID-19">COVID-19</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-185" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-185">&#91;185&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
